  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_1c45e10f-3142-4e5d-ab2d-cf34e62dd558'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer6764361002931315798">For Annie Phillips, there is a right way to do things and everything has a place. College and her flawless GPA are top priority, as is planning her perfect future. Anything less than perfection is unacceptable. So when she meets Loden Guiles, she believes she has finally found her perfect happily-ever-after.<br/> <br/>Chase Malloy is funny, loyal, and an all around nice guy. He’s al</span>
  <span id="freeText6764361002931315798" style="display:none">For Annie Phillips, there is a right way to do things and everything has a place. College and her flawless GPA are top priority, as is planning her perfect future. Anything less than perfection is unacceptable. So when she meets Loden Guiles, she believes she has finally found her perfect happily-ever-after.<br /> <br />Chase Malloy is funny, loyal, and an all around nice guy. He’s also sloppy, tattooed, and undirected. All Chase wants to do is survive college, hang out with friends, and make music. Knowing his best friend’s step-sister since they were fourteen, Annie and he have always had a love-hate relationship. The last thing Chase expects is to fall for Annie, but he knows he’ll never live up to her idea of the perfect man.<br /> <br />On the outside, Annie and Loden’s relationship appears picture perfect. But behind closed doors, Annie quickly realizes Loden isn’t the man he pretends to be. Every time her not so well laid plans crumble, and Loden proves to be not so Mr. Right, Chase is there to pick her up and brush her off. Will she realize the perfection she’s been searching for has been in front of her all this time?<br /><br />*Long After is a companion novel to Sometimes Never and Before Now. Many of the same characters appear in Chase and Annie's story. However, it can be read as a stand-alone book.<br /><br />**This is a new adult novel. Due to harsh language, sexual situations, and violence, this book is recommended for 17+.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer676966015" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10385523691563547123">5 stars<br/><br/><a href='http://s1274.photobucket.com/albums/y432/RReadoholic/?action=view&current=1E7B99BB-6AFF-48BF-AFCF-BD4DD8BE5340-160-0000001902E2D278_zps291745c1.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382546803i/5977896._SY540_.jpg' alt='Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>My <b>all time favourite</b> storyline when the couple starts off with a <b>love-hate </b>relationship. Annie and Chase have been friends for years and now off to college.<br/><br/>What I loved the most about this book is Chase. He was <b>cheeky, protective</b>, <b>laid back. </b>The banter between the main characters was cute and funny.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>You want to shove things up my ass?...I didn't know you were so kinky</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>Okay, </b>so there was a few things that didn't go down well with me. A couple times I wanted the story to get </span>
  <span id="freeText10385523691563547123" style="display:none">5 stars<br><br><a href="http://s1274.photobucket.com/albums/y432/RReadoholic/?action=view&amp;current=1E7B99BB-6AFF-48BF-AFCF-BD4DD8BE5340-160-0000001902E2D278_zps291745c1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382546803i/5977896._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>My <b>all time favourite</b> storyline when the couple starts off with a <b>love-hate </b>relationship. Annie and Chase have been friends for years and now off to college.<br><br>What I loved the most about this book is Chase. He was <b>cheeky, protective</b>, <b>laid back. </b>The banter between the main characters was cute and funny.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>You want to shove things up my ass?...I didn't know you were so kinky</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Okay, </b>so there was a few things that didn't go down well with me. A couple times I wanted the story to get back to the present sooner. And when it did I felt it <b>ended too abruptly. </b>Annie started off a strong heroine but slowly she dipped with <b>her decision making. </b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I was willing to wait on you long before you had a reason to take your time. I think Im willing to wait long after</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I will still give this 5 stars because I was getting serious <b>butterflies in my stomach, </b>I was <b>swooning hard for Chase, </b> the romance was <b>dragged out</b> just how I like it, <b>I loved the writing style</b>and just because I'm a hopeless romantic that <b>loves friends-to-lovers </b>books. If you like the above, I would give this book a go x<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="10385523691563547123" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Sunniva Dee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/19081557-sunniva-dee"><img alt="Sunniva Dee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442896793p2/19081557.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/730091573?book_show_action=true">Sep 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sunniva Dee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sunniva Dee" href="/user/show/19081557-sunniva-dee">Sunniva Dee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19081557-sunniva-dee?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer730091573" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11571303025765378943">Let me start by saying that once you've discovered Cheryl McIntyre and her books, you're sold. At least, that's what it was like for me. Dark Calling, then starting with the series of stand-alone books that are still connected character-wise—Sometimes Never, Blackbird, and Before Now—they're all incredible reads. Now, with Long After, Cheryl is simply settling in among the very top New Adult authors in this country. Step aside you bigger names that I will not mention because I am polite. ;-)<br/><br/>I ha</span>
  <span id="freeText11571303025765378943" style="display:none">Let me start by saying that once you've discovered Cheryl McIntyre and her books, you're sold. At least, that's what it was like for me. Dark Calling, then starting with the series of stand-alone books that are still connected character-wise—Sometimes Never, Blackbird, and Before Now—they're all incredible reads. Now, with Long After, Cheryl is simply settling in among the very top New Adult authors in this country. Step aside you bigger names that I will not mention because I am polite. ;-)<br /><br />I have a couple of pet peeves (besides bad writing, of course); poor or unrealistic character development, and illogical occurrences throughout a book. Cheryl never, ever falls into those traps. With Long After, I had the honor of beta reading, and if anyone has seen Casey Ford's review of Long After, I'm still doing exactly what he paints so vividly for us there.<br /><br />In my case, I was on a deadline with my manuscript. The goal was to read Long After between editing and writing, but as always with Cheryl's novels, the plan was null and void as soon as I started reading. YES, it's passionate, YES, it's real, believable, and YES, the love story is so breathtaking, heart-wrenching and hopeful all at once that it's impossible to put the darn thing down once you start reading. So fair warning, guys. &lt;3<br /><br />As I've mentioned in another review: Annie and Chase are painted so vividly and in such a realistic way that I wouldn't have been surprised if I ran into them on the street. I would probably have recognized them by the way they looked at each other.<br /><br />Again, congratulations on another beautiful book, Cheryl. Already, I can't wait for the next one.<br />xoxo<br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beth Michele" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beth Michele" href="/user/show/16809610-beth-michele">Beth Michele</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer652743467" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer66877032546651202">Let me start out by saying that I love Cheryl McIntyre's books and will read anything she writes. That said, I honestly didn't think it was possible for her to get any more fantastic...and then I read Long After.<br/><br/>In some ways, this book seemed to reach deeper than her other novels. I initially thought it might be a light read, but it was anything but. I loved learning more about Chase and Annie, both damaged in their own ways, most specifically Annie. While in the other novels it appears she has </span>
  <span id="freeText66877032546651202" style="display:none">Let me start out by saying that I love Cheryl McIntyre's books and will read anything she writes. That said, I honestly didn't think it was possible for her to get any more fantastic...and then I read Long After.<br /><br />In some ways, this book seemed to reach deeper than her other novels. I initially thought it might be a light read, but it was anything but. I loved learning more about Chase and Annie, both damaged in their own ways, most specifically Annie. While in the other novels it appears she has no feelings and is just a cold shell of a human being, we discover in Long After that, that couldn't be far from the truth. She has a heart of gold and soon discovers that Chase does as well.<br /><br />As always, Cheryl manages to endear each and every character in the story to me. She makes me smile, laugh, cry, and always feel better for having read one of her novels, a piece of it lingering in my heart.<br /><br />I fell completely and totally in love with Chase, and, after discovering what Annie was truly made of, she stole a chunk of my heart as well.<br /><br />There are many lines from the novel that I could quote, but the one that summed it up for me and says it best is this:<br /><br />"Chase is definitely out of my comfort zone. He's also, ironically, the person I feel safest with. My highest connection. My home. And sometimes, you just need to go home."<br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_737168843" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/737168843" />
    <a title="Holly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9625203-holly"><img alt="Holly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1410368956p2/9625203.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/737168843?book_show_action=true">Oct 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Holly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Holly" href="/user/show/9625203-holly">Holly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer737168843" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16379899110970330505">Before now, Before Now was my favorite of Cheryl's, however, Long After has unequivocally replaced it as my favorite book of hers. The writing was spectacular, after the preface and first chapter alone my heart was already beating faster in anticipation of what was to come and I was ready to cry. Or find Xanax. Chase and Annie's story pulled me in from the beginning. I liked the history these two had together. I really loved their sarcastic banter.. A personal favorite...Chase to Annie upon seei</span>
  <span id="freeText16379899110970330505" style="display:none">Before now, Before Now was my favorite of Cheryl's, however, Long After has unequivocally replaced it as my favorite book of hers. The writing was spectacular, after the preface and first chapter alone my heart was already beating faster in anticipation of what was to come and I was ready to cry. Or find Xanax. Chase and Annie's story pulled me in from the beginning. I liked the history these two had together. I really loved their sarcastic banter.. A personal favorite...Chase to Annie upon seeing her talking to another guy..<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"So anyway," I say loudly. "Make sure you get checked. Shaving doesn't get rid of them. That's a myth. You need the special shampoo." I nod at Todd and scratch my crotch for good measure. "See you later." "Uh...later."</i>
</b><br /><br />I liked Annie, I understood her need for perfection. I know what it's like to feel like anything less than your absolute best is a fate worse than death. I related to her control-freak ways. A LOT! <br /><br /><b>
  <i>"There is a wrong way to do a task, and then there's a right way- my way. And it bothers me when people don't perform a task in the way I would. Bother may not be the correct word, either. It's like watching someone purposely walk into a burning building."</i>
</b><br /><br />AMEN if more people did things our way the world would be a better place!!!<br /><br />Chase however, stole my heart in this book. He was an absolute amazing friend to Annie throughout the entire story. Every single one of his actions showed just how much he loved her even before he realized he was in love with her. Even when she was together with "that other guy" (I can't even say his name, saying his name riles me up and gets me all kinds of mad. I hated him. Like if he was on fire I wouldn't pee on him to put him out unless I peed diesel fuel hated him) and pushed Chase away, he was still there for her whenever she needed someone. He NEVER left her hanging; he was the definition of knight in shining armor...hot, sexy, armor to boot :-)<br /><br />You can draw your own conclusions based on the synopsis and warning about what subject matter is included in the story. To go into it, I feel like it would take away some of the emotions I want to you experience first hand like I did. Chase &amp; Annie's story will make you feel. It threw me on the emotional roller coaster complete with upside down loops and all! It's a heartbreaking, panic, gasp inducing story at times but at other times it's a beautiful love story between two people finally realizing what was in front of them all along. Cheryl has such an amazing way of bringing her characters to life and getting them deep under your skin where weeks and months later you're still thinking about them. Without a doubt she has become one of my MUST read authors. You will NOT be disappointed with her.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16379899110970330505" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer695591123" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16474224152849206392">Ohhhhhh myyyyyyyyyy goddddddddd...Ms. Cheryl McIntyre welcome to my fave authors circle! This one's gonna be a gusher peeps. Seriously. Simply written but nonetheless a really beautiful relationship is woven into this story. What I like about her novels is that although the growth of the featured relationship plays a key role in the novel, it's not the book. It's embedded within a solid story and is really character driven. Start with good characters and you have the basis of something special. </span>
  <span id="freeText16474224152849206392" style="display:none">Ohhhhhh myyyyyyyyyy goddddddddd...Ms. Cheryl McIntyre welcome to my fave authors circle! This one's gonna be a gusher peeps. Seriously. Simply written but nonetheless a really beautiful relationship is woven into this story. What I like about her novels is that although the growth of the featured relationship plays a key role in the novel, it's not the book. It's embedded within a solid story and is really character driven. Start with good characters and you have the basis of something special. And, I think CM is damn good at pulling this off. Reading one of her novels is like heaven for me - expertly written heroines and males, both as supporting or as her protagonists.<br /><br />Even though her females struggle, the way they fight is admirable and strong. Real with setbacks but also real with personal wins as well. A nicely balanced portrayal.<br /><br />Chase is quite possibly my favourite character in this series that just straight up kicks ass! I love well-written characters and the dynamic that he has with Annie is perfect. You see why they have a connection, it's not told to you and you're not beaten over the head with it, it just is. Their chemistry is a great mix of comedic "insults" (especially the one involving bestiality, lol)and then real substance so that their relationship doesn't come off as irritating and angsty. Rather it flows naturally as they both grow individually.<br /><br />Especially Annie, I enjoyed watching her let go and learn to receive the love she's given as she fights to be happy. Her struggle in this novel is handled really well. I felt ill for her and just wanted to jump through the pages in the final confrontation. <br /><br />What also elevated this story for me was CM's effective use of flash backs and flash forwards. It really told this story well <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[and I found the 2nd flash forward in conjunction with the one in the prologue to be especially impactful. We find out exactly what went down in that first scene before it actually comes to fruition in the climax toward the end where we get the full experience. That flash forward hits you hard in the heartwrench dept. The portrayal of Annie's abusive relationship is disturbing and I have to say gets to you, as a woman. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br />And the bonus scene - holy shit, that was an excellent way to finish the book even though it wasn't the official wrap up. You'll see what I mean! Just please pick this series up and you won't be sorry and for those who have read the previous books, then you should be falling all over yourselves trying to get it. I can't wait for anything this woman writes!<br /><br />UPDATE***<br />Almost forgot to mention, the use of music and specific songs that Chase uses to communicate to Annie throughout the novel - f'n genius! Told ya it was gonna be a gusher ;)</span>
  <a data-text-id="16474224152849206392" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/663770585" />
    <a title="Holly Baker" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15948101-holly-baker"><img alt="Holly Baker" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1522326241p2/15948101.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/663770585?book_show_action=true">Jul 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Holly Baker" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Holly Baker" href="/user/show/15948101-holly-baker">Holly Baker</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5118435583033864113">****ARC received in exchange for an honest review****<br/><br/><b>Nobody is perfect until you fall in love with them.</b><br/><br/>Wow! What a freaking book! I didn't think it was possible to love this book more than Before Now (Park's book) but I think that just happened. Long After was so much more than I was expecting and had me up until 4am in an almost constant mixed state of happy and heartbreak. So much went on in this book that it was just impossible to put down because I was desperate to find out how it all came </span>
  <span id="freeText5118435583033864113" style="display:none">****ARC received in exchange for an honest review****<br /><br /><b>Nobody is perfect until you fall in love with them.</b><br /><br />Wow! What a freaking book! I didn't think it was possible to love this book more than Before Now (Park's book) but I think that just happened. Long After was so much more than I was expecting and had me up until 4am in an almost constant mixed state of happy and heartbreak. So much went on in this book that it was just impossible to put down because I was desperate to find out how it all came together. <br /><br />In Sometimes Never (#1), Blackbird (#1.5) and Before Now (#2) I wasn't exactly a fan of Annie. Hope had nicknamed her "Princess Bitch" and i think we can all agree that was very fitting. But literally as soon as I started reading Long After, I completely changed my opinion on her. There are reasons she acted how she did and that, along with what she deals with in Long After, makes your feelings about her do a complete 180. <br /><br /><b>"I was willing to wait on you long before you had a reason to take your time. I think I'm willing to wait long after."</b><br /><br />Also... I just cheated on Park with Chase. I love Park SO much but Chase put up one heck of a fight to win my heart. He's funny, gorgeous, caring, tattooed, plays the bass, and have you <i>seen</i> that cover picture???? Swooooooon! I also love that the cover is fitting to the book. Chase is a swimmer and as you can see, the lovely Richard Rocco is glistening with water on the cover and looking oh so sexy!<br /><br /><b>"Good," I say. "Because regardless of my name, with this hard-on, I really don't think I could chase you."</b><br /><br />This book started off exactly how I was expecting. Fantastic, fun, addictive, and so funny I laughed out loud too many times to count. And then Cheryl completely changed it up. It got <i>intense</i> and I was not expecting the subject matter that arose. Cue the tears. It was heartbreaking and the way it was all delivered to the reader, I honestly had no idea how it was going to end.<br /><br />I was so miserable when the book ended. Not because the ending was bad. It was <i>amazing!</i> The beginning, middle, end, and everything in between wad amazing. But I was so in love with Annie and Chase's story and I wasn't ready to let them go. I could honestly read about this group of characters for years to come because they are one of my very favourite fictional families and I love each and every one of them. <br /><br /><b>"I have feelings for someone," I blurt. He regards me with an amused smirk. His blue eyes twinkle - I swear. "What kind of feelings are we talking about? Like, tingly-in-the-pants feelings? Or wedding-invitation-in-the-mail feelings?"</b><br /><br />Long After was simply perfect and the fact that the amazing Cheryl McIntyre even treated us to a bonus scene just made me love it even more. You really don't want to miss out on this book. Once again, the Sometimes Never series gets 5 stars from me. <br /><br /><b>"Worth the wait," he says adamantly. "Well worth it."</b></span>

<div id="review_737043418" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/737043418" />
    <a title="Heather" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21642617-heather"><img alt="Heather" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1383334480p2/21642617.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/737043418?book_show_action=true">Oct 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Heather" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heather" href="/user/show/21642617-heather">Heather</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21642617-heather?shelf=strong-heroine">strong-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21642617-heather?shelf=find-more-by-author">find-more-by-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21642617-heather?shelf=readoverandoveragain">readoverandoveragain</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21642617-heather?shelf=sequel-coming">sequel-coming</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21642617-heather?shelf=funny-romance">funny-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21642617-heather?shelf=book-boyfriend">book-boyfriend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21642617-heather?shelf=tear-jerker">tear-jerker</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21642617-heather?shelf=beyond-normal-na">beyond-normal-na</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21642617-heather?shelf=emotional-roller-coaster">emotional-roller-coaster</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21642617-heather?shelf=all-time-favorite">all-time-favorite</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer737043418" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3262900241860812483">This book is going to go way up to the top of my favorites list. Here's a few non-spoiler reasons why:<br/>1. It's not overloaded with drama and angst. So many of the newer NA books seem to have a need to just fill it with all these really messed up pasts. Long After doesn't have that. In fact, Chase wasn't screwed up at all - AND both his parents were still together AND he isn't the local man whore who disrespects women AND he isn't a druggie alcoholic AND <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ not only is he not violent/</span></span>
  <span id="freeText3262900241860812483" style="display:none">This book is going to go way up to the top of my favorites list. Here's a few non-spoiler reasons why:<br />1. It's not overloaded with drama and angst. So many of the newer NA books seem to have a need to just fill it with all these really messed up pasts. Long After doesn't have that. In fact, Chase wasn't screwed up at all - AND both his parents were still together AND he isn't the local man whore who disrespects women AND he isn't a druggie alcoholic AND <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ not only is he not violent/stalker - there is a character who is - and the female lead DOESN'T end up with him.  spoiler&gt;. I wonder if they will strip the NA category away since it breaks from the template of norm?<br />2. It addresses real-life issues in such a way that it can appeal to any woman, since we have either been there ourselves or knew someone who was. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ there are predator men like Loden everywhere. And so many women have low self esteem for whatever reason. Once in a relationship like that, it is so hard to recognize how bad it is, since it creeps up. And you do question whether it was somehow your fault - and usually believe it to be so, it is easy to look in from the outside and judge. It is easy to say no man will ever lay his hands on me. Then it happens. This book carries the reader through all of it. Anyone in this situation will not only relate, but I do believe it could even help them in knowing they are not alone. And there is a way out.<br />3. Minimal Sex. This is an odd one, because I labeled it as a steamy novel, yet there wasn't that much in it. That's because even though it wasn't hit and heavy, it is still one of the most intimate books I've ever read, the friendship, the phone calls, the different songs every night - that's what will last. And that's what ultimately saved her.<br /> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />4.the pranks on each other<br />5. The updates on the other characters, without it seeming like a continuation. I so really tired of all these 'to be continued' books. This series is not like that at all, as each could stand on its own, but if you have read them, it's like running into an old friend at the store. Happy to see them and get an update, but don't plan to hang with them all the time.<br />6. Post it notes <br /><br />Wish I could go higher than 5 stars, as it is really that good.<br /><br />I could only think of one downside/dislike or maybe just complete confusion. What in the hell we're Chase, Park, and Guy playing hide and go seek in the dark, with only the 3 of them. So weird, if I had been in Annie's shoes at that moment, I would have turned and left and not gone back in.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>
  <a data-text-id="3262900241860812483" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText15614946038018392254" style="display:none">Omg I taught Hope's story was my favorite. Then I was pretty sure Parks story stole that title. BUT I was wrong! Chase ans Annie's one is the winner of the top spot!!!! I always taught Annie was a bitch I'm not gonna lie. And to be honest she is lol. BUT has has a heart of gold,you just have to get passed the bitchyness to see that. This book starts off somewhere I won't say where but it's dark,then goes back 27 months to see how we got there. She meets Chase when she's 14,been the friend of her step brother Guy. She instantly likes him. And he hardly notices her. So she gets it in to her head that she's not gonna give him the time of day. This begins there Bitchy 6 year love/hate relationship. But there's a fine line between love and hate,been on the same side of the coin. Chase loves to annoy her as much as she loves to be bitchy to him though,as you see from the start of the book. Even in college now this continues. Now Chase isn't blind,he thinks Annie is HOT(well he is a hot blooded male!) But she's Guy's sister. And he doesn't want anything to happen with her....Right? That's Okay until someone else has there eye's on Annie. Enter Lodan. Douche bag of the century. Ugh I really don't get what was going through her head with him. But hey who am I to judge :) This relationship is like a tipping point in a hole domino collapse. Leading you up to where the book starts. This book has so many highs and lows you will love it. I loved them and I hated them. I wanted to smack Annie and I wanted to comfort her. I wanted to dig Lodan in the face and I wanted to.....No wait I always just wanted to inflict pain on him LOL I won't say more about it because I want everyone to read the book spoiler free. But I can tell you this you will love it. You will fall in love with Chase and Annie as much as I did. OH and another bonus was seen Hope and Park! Ugh loved seen them :) Please when this book goes live GET IT! Cheryl's books are so good everyone should see :) </span>

<div id="review_747961002" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/747961002" />
    <a title="Kelli C " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14931216-kelli-c"><img alt="Kelli C " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1426900480p2/14931216.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/747961002?book_show_action=true">Oct 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kelli C " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kelli C " href="/user/show/14931216-kelli-c">Kelli C </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer747961002" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16547701761657732875">Long After is by far my fave of this series. I am a sucker for charming witty banter coupled with a bit of angst and in your face love that shocks the hell out of everyone when it is realized! I also like damaged characters that truly grow and find the inner strength to go after what they want for themselves. Cheryl McIntyre has nailed of those things for me in one book.<br/><br/>Chase Malloy is a fine specimen of man, with the perfect boyish charm that cannot be denied. He has that perfect boy next door </span>
  <span id="freeText16547701761657732875" style="display:none">Long After is by far my fave of this series. I am a sucker for charming witty banter coupled with a bit of angst and in your face love that shocks the hell out of everyone when it is realized! I also like damaged characters that truly grow and find the inner strength to go after what they want for themselves. Cheryl McIntyre has nailed of those things for me in one book.<br /><br />Chase Malloy is a fine specimen of man, with the perfect boyish charm that cannot be denied. He has that perfect boy next door attitude yet he has off the charts sex appeal. He is strong, loyal and dependable...everything Annie needs in her life, yet doesnt know. Poor Annie...what a train wreck! She is living in her world of control, avoiding any chaos. She is just looking for a way to have a perfect life and to be taken care of, however her quest leads her to be stuck in a relationship with an absolute monster defined by rage and jealousy! I had many breath holding moments wondering is Annie was gonna be breathing at the end of the scene! Enter Chase, her longtime "friend" and pain in the ass constant. He is determined to keep her safe and keep her as his own no matter how resistant Annie is. But one night can change so much...it can change the heart, it can change the mind, and it can change one's life forever.<br /><br />I loved these characters. Together they are constantly busting balls and wrecking havoc on each other's minds and hearts. Chase's character was written so well...he was so real and so good that i wanted to yell "save me"!!!! Annie, although a bit weak was surprisingly not annoying. She was never needy or whiny, she just basically existed until her scenes with Chase brought her character to life! There are so many good things to say about this book, but i dont give spoilers away. I know that i will forever love "sticky notes" and the amazing way they can change your life! </span>
  <a data-text-id="16547701761657732875" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText16409313772301700970" style="display:none"><br><b>Not enough stars...</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385031906i/7053026.jpg" alt="..." class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>LOVED this book. Don't know how i missed it but I'm so glad i was able to read it sooner than later...Thanks for recommending it Julia. I.<br>This was the third book in the series but was told that it could be read as a stand alone, even though the characters played a small part in the first two books. <br>Thank you for writing this beautiful story Cheryl McIntyre. The writing was exquisite....The anguish, the desire, the raw subject, the heart trembling moments, the chemistry, the build up, the tension (boy talk about tension), the humor, and our favorite, love....It was all there in just the right amounts. Sad that it had to end...please keep writing and can't wait to read the Kellin and Misty's story.<br><br>Just a few things i loved about the book: LOVED: Author picking odd numbers describing time line in the beginning, middle, than even at the end...don't know if it meant anything to her but for me it matched the story line, and thought it was very clever. LOVED: The cheeseburger scene, LOVED it, it was HOT and funny at the same time. LOVED: The post-it notes, i thought that was so incredibly sweet. LOVED: A bonus scene that you don't want to miss. <br><br>Such a great and a memorable tale. </span>

<div id="review_743323558" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/743323558" />
    <a title="Book Junky Girls" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24411646-book-junky-girls"><img alt="Book Junky Girls" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1458139559p2/24411646.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/743323558?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Book Junky Girls" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Book Junky Girls" href="/user/show/24411646-book-junky-girls">Book Junky Girls</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer743323558" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5593907134385378288"><b>4.5 STARS!</b><br/><br/>The long anticipated story of Annie and Chase. <br/><br/>And it was worth the wait. Annie was always seen as the Barbie bitch so seeing how things really are from her POV gives you the answers to questions you didn't even know you had. <br/><br/>Chase has always had the good guy persona, but he didn't have his life figured out. You see him finally come together and figure out what he really wants in himself and in life.<br/><br/> Annie's story made me am emotional mess at times, seeing the pain she went through, bu</span>
  <span id="freeText5593907134385378288" style="display:none"><b>4.5 STARS!</b><br /><br />The long anticipated story of Annie and Chase. <br /><br />And it was worth the wait. Annie was always seen as the Barbie bitch so seeing how things really are from her POV gives you the answers to questions you didn't even know you had. <br /><br />Chase has always had the good guy persona, but he didn't have his life figured out. You see him finally come together and figure out what he really wants in himself and in life.<br /><br /> Annie's story made me am emotional mess at times, seeing the pain she went through, but didn't allow anyone else to see. <br /><br />After all the hardships she endures seeing her pick herself back up and put herself back together, with help from Chase. Her growth throughout the book even after everything that she went through was inspirational. <br /><br /> Chase is definitely swoon worthy and his patience with Annie was so sweet. I loved how he knew her well enough not to push her while still pushing her. <br /><br />Great read I've loved the entire series and although I still have a special spot for Mason, Chase has surpassed him in the book boyfriend arena for me.<br /><br /><br /><br /><br />Annie got her happily ever after and Chase adores her. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5593907134385378288" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_745466399" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/745466399" />
    <a title="Ermani" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7209059-ermani"><img alt="Ermani" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1604717233p2/7209059.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/745466399?book_show_action=true">Oct 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ermani" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ermani" href="/user/show/7209059-ermani">Ermani</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer745466399" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16506731313357706626">4.5. Minor Spoilers<br/>As much as we love our alphas, I am glad when a book brings to light domestic violence involving young women. As our younger single readers look at these jealous possessive types and love them on paper, there is a fine line in the real world when someone may be displaying signs of future abuse. Just like our heroine, it starts small and grows with women making excuses for their partner leading to feeling trapped and insecure. A strong man who knows what he wants and isn't afra</span>
  <span id="freeText16506731313357706626" style="display:none">4.5. Minor Spoilers<br />As much as we love our alphas, I am glad when a book brings to light domestic violence involving young women. As our younger single readers look at these jealous possessive types and love them on paper, there is a fine line in the real world when someone may be displaying signs of future abuse. Just like our heroine, it starts small and grows with women making excuses for their partner leading to feeling trapped and insecure. A strong man who knows what he wants and isn't afraid to say it is a really great thing. But it's important for women to know who is actually giving a girl red flags.<br /><br />Loved this book. I thought Annie was very well written. I enjoyed seeing inside her head at how the abuse was affecting her. Chase was beautifully written. It showed how a friend can brush aside signs as well and not know what to do to help. Loved Chase and Annie together. Took awhile but it was worth the wait. This book wasn't overly heavy despite the subject matter but managed to bring about key points that I'm glad to see. Time jumps were occasionally confusing. That's my only criticism. Great read, loved it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16506731313357706626" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_757760442" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/757760442" />
    <a title="Kathryn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22870496-kathryn"><img alt="Kathryn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1389491595p2/22870496.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/757760442?book_show_action=true">Nov 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kathryn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kathryn" href="/user/show/22870496-kathryn">Kathryn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer757760442" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4872601880937387667">Started this book this morning at work, and rushed home to finish it in one sitting. I was just looking for a quick read to get me through my work day - wasn't expecting to find such a gem! I usually don't read books with characters in this age range (20-21) but WOW. Just wow. I absolutely ADORED Chase. He melted my heart over and over again. I didn't like the heroine, Annie at first and almost wanted to give this book four stars because of it. But as I continued reading and thinking, I applaud </span>
  <span id="freeText4872601880937387667" style="display:none">Started this book this morning at work, and rushed home to finish it in one sitting. I was just looking for a quick read to get me through my work day - wasn't expecting to find such a gem! I usually don't read books with characters in this age range (20-21) but WOW. Just wow. I absolutely ADORED Chase. He melted my heart over and over again. I didn't like the heroine, Annie at first and almost wanted to give this book four stars because of it. But as I continued reading and thinking, I applaud Cheryl because I think she portrayed physical and emotional abuse in a real and raw way. I grew to love Annie as she matured and reading how Chase changed her for the better. <br /><br />I also LOVED the storyline and timeline of this book. Some romances tend to annoy me because the relationships seem so rushed and unrealistic. This book took place over several months and Chase and Annie's love bloomed gradually. This book was wonderfully written - highly recommend for anyone looking for a quick, emotional, and well-written read. Now I have the urge to go buy a bunch of Post It's.....</span>
  <a data-text-id="4872601880937387667" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

I loved Sometime Never and I loved Before Now even more. I didn’t think those books can be topped. But there you have it … Long After is the BEST. The story of Chase and Annie. An emotional roller coaster, beautiful and compelling. Ms. McIntyre you are a great storyteller.</span>

<div id="review_738852352" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/738852352" />
    <a title="Victoria S." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16806019-victoria-s"><img alt="Victoria S." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1409062313p2/16806019.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/738852352?book_show_action=true">Oct 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Victoria S." class="user" itemprop="url" name="Victoria S." href="/user/show/16806019-victoria-s">Victoria S.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16806019-victoria-s?shelf=reread-again">reread-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16806019-victoria-s?shelf=got-to-have">got-to-have</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16806019-victoria-s?shelf=author-on-to-watch-list">author-on-to-watch-list</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16806019-victoria-s?shelf=can-t-wait-for-rest-of-series">can-t-wait-for-rest-of-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16806019-victoria-s?shelf=amazballs-of-series">amazballs-of-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer738852352" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13695873967418522821">4.5 Stars Story You'll Love Long After Reading!!<br/><br/>Ms. McIntyre has out done herself with Chase and Annie’s story. For those of you who have read the two previous books in the Sometimes Never series, you’ve seen the glimpses we’ve gotten of Chase and Annie in both Sometimes Never and Before Now. Chase has always came off as the carefree intriguing jackass jokester and Annie the uptight, insecure, pain in the characters’ asses. These two characters have always engaged in funny banter nick picking at</span>
  <span id="freeText13695873967418522821" style="display:none">4.5 Stars Story You'll Love Long After Reading!!<br><br>Ms. McIntyre has out done herself with Chase and Annie’s story. For those of you who have read the two previous books in the Sometimes Never series, you’ve seen the glimpses we’ve gotten of Chase and Annie in both Sometimes Never and Before Now. Chase has always came off as the carefree intriguing jackass jokester and Annie the uptight, insecure, pain in the characters’ asses. These two characters have always engaged in funny banter nick picking at one another, fussing, and fighting. We continues to see these characteristics and interactions over the course of the story but we get such an in-depth look into these two thinking process. The book is told in both POVs which is extremely enjoyable to see how each other perceives one another’s flaws and see the turmoil both endure in terms of their feelings for one another. The prologue is told present tense then chapter one back tracks us to 27months prior the journey is rocky with swerves, curves, and a big crash so buckle up.<br><br>Where Mason attracted you, Parker hooked you, Chase will steal your heart. He is an upfront, genuinely honest guy, loyal friend.<br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/105870753@N07/10727052924/" title="Chase from Long After by vshriver303, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383844957i/6682928._SY540_.jpg" width="480" height="720" alt="Chase from Long After" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>What you see with Chase is what you get. He isn’t prefect by any means but you can appreciate his trueness to himself, he doesn’t claim nor tries to be anyone but him. Chase not only puts up with and looks after Annie because he’s best friends with her brother Guy, or because he’s her friend rather <br><br><i>
  <b>"It's not friendship I feel for Annie, though I think it's safe to say she's my best friend."</b>
</i><br><br>The way Chase is protective of Annie is beyond heartwarming. Where he gets weary and steers clear of openly admitting his feelings, he communicates through songs he plays for her to listen (Has he met Remy? Ahh sigh love this action by a guy). <br><br>Annie has encountered her troubles stemming from Sometimes Never when Hope beats the crap out of jerk off football player who throws Annie to curb as if trash after sleeping with her. So to say her self-esteem has been hurting for a while is an understatement. I think a lot of us girls/woman can relate to Annie. When we feel insecure or defensive we put up a shield and give off that “bitch vibe” same goes for Annie.<br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/105870753@N07/10727123095/" title="Annie from Long After by vshriver303, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383844957i/6682929._SY540_.jpg" width="640" height="640" alt="Annie from Long After" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Annie not only suffers from her OCD tendencies she also strives head strong for perfection; but in her pursuit she doesn’t respect herself and rather expects so much less what she deserves. Prime Example---Loden. Holy kickboxing gloves filled with concrete how I’d love to knock this guy into another galaxy. You know that scum you get on your shoes from walking around city streets, while this guy is 10x scummier than that. <br><br>Cheryl McIntyre touches on a very present and serious issue that takes place in everyday relationships; the way she discusses it is vulnerably real. Both characters grow so much over the course of the story. They help one another grow individually and together. <br><br><i>
  <b>“There’s this way we touch—deliberately, tenderly, secretly—that puts us into some category I don’t have a name for.”</b>
</i><br><br>The progression takes times which gradually has you scooting closer to the edge of your seat, as they inch closer to opening up to inch closer to coming off your seat, you just want to know when these two will finally confess their feelings WHEN?? Annie is broken, scared, and unconfident but Chases is the perfect balance, he is patient, strong, and knows what he wants.<br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/105870753@N07/10728189654/" title="Long After by vshriver303, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383844957i/6682930._SX540_.jpg" width="600" height="439" alt="Long After" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Loved the flash blacks and flash forwards keeps your attentions grasped you need to know What Happened/What is going to Happen. About 70% into story you anticipate what is going to happen but still doesn’t deter you from finishing makes you push further even farther. Grab your pom poms you will become Chase’s cheerleader. <br><br>Amazing story with such relatable characters. Well done Ms. McIntyre I cannot wait for the next in the series One more please just to wrap all three couples stories up. Would love to have Guy’s story he is the glue in every story, while his presence isn’t shone under the spotlight he helps everyone come together.<br><br>P.S. Ladies Idk you but if there were a store that sold hot guys as decorations Chase would be my 1st purchase!<br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/105870753@N07/10728212606/" title="Chase Decorations by vshriver303, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383844957i/6682931._SY540_.jpg" width="720" height="834" alt="Chase Decorations" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13695873967418522821" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_670134555" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/670134555" />
    <a title="Danielle " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11938713-danielle"><img alt="Danielle " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1524409963p2/11938713.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/670134555?book_show_action=true">Jul 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Danielle " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Danielle " href="/user/show/11938713-danielle">Danielle </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer670134555" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1133016243607608126">5 stars<br/><br/>Every time I read a Cheryl McIntyre book I am convinced she just wrote by favorite book and then I read the next one she writes and that one instantly becomes my favorite. There is so much emotion and deep, strong story lines in this books. She is not afraid to touch on issues that others might shy away from. The way she tells the story is so amazing you feel like you are going through the story firsthand hand. All of her books have sucked me in so much I can not put them down. I have to </span>
  <span id="freeText1133016243607608126" style="display:none">5 stars<br /><br />Every time I read a Cheryl McIntyre book I am convinced she just wrote by favorite book and then I read the next one she writes and that one instantly becomes my favorite. There is so much emotion and deep, strong story lines in this books. She is not afraid to touch on issues that others might shy away from. The way she tells the story is so amazing you feel like you are going through the story firsthand hand. All of her books have sucked me in so much I can not put them down. I have to keep reading. That is when you know what you are reading is an incredible story. Well for me at least. <br /><br />Chase Malloy is a college student, who if you read the other books in this series, in a integral part of the core group. He has been friends with the same people most of his life. While things in all of their lives change, they all seem to always be close knit. He has also been in love with one of them for as long as her can remember. Annie Phillips. She is the the beautiful high school cheerleader turned beautiful college student/nemesis. Rather than admit this two feel something for each other, they constantly are taking jabs at each other. While super funny at times, you can also feel the attraction between the two of them.<br /><br />For some reason, the timing for these two to get together is always off. They can never seem to get their feelings out to the other person in the right time. One of them is always dating someone else. Just as Chase is finally going to say something to Annie, she meets Loden. Annie thinks Loden is perfect. He is smart, good looking, wealthy, everything she is looking for. Annie has a crazy theory that she doesn't want to end up like her mom. Her mom has been married 3 times and all her kids have different dads. This is not what Annie wants for her life. She is determined that she will not end up like her mom. She wants her life organized and with one person for the rest of her life. Stability is key for her. <br /><br />Loden turns out to be far from perfect. He is jealous, possessive and abusive. Annie somehow feels like she can stick with this relationship. One night Chase finds out that Loden is hurting Annie. She makes him keep her secret and not tell anyone else what is going on. Chase agrees but only if Annie checks in with him every day. Chase doesn't feel good about keeping Annie's secret, but does it because he doesn't want her to cut herself off from everyone. <br /><br />Chase talking to Annie every night for the "check ins" not only keep Chase in contact with Annie but it brings them closer. Talking for hours on the phone or hanging out is what makes them happy. Chase realizes he is falling in love with Annie and deep down inside Annie knows she is falling for Chase. She is afraid of leaving Loden. She is afraid of what will happen if she is with Chase. He is chaos. She needs order and her life in a neat package. <br /><br />This book was amazing. I love this whole series. Each book is just as emotional yet engaging as the one before it. While this book is part of a series, it can be read alone. There are the same characters in all books. Loved seeing what everyone was doing as the times passes. If you have not read the other books, you MUST!!! </span>
  <a data-text-id="1133016243607608126" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_734042880" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/734042880" />
    <a title="Lustful Literature" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24150778-lustful-literature"><img alt="Lustful Literature" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1379863713p2/24150778.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/734042880?book_show_action=true">Oct 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lustful Literature" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lustful Literature" href="/user/show/24150778-lustful-literature">Lustful Literature</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer734042880" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10370995915490907106"><b>*4.5 stars*<br/><br/>**SHANYN’S REVIEW**</b><br/><br/>I have never read a book by this author before, and after reading this one, I definitely plan on reading the others.<br/><br/>Annie and Chase are wonderful together, they have such great chemistry, and I was drawn in right from the start.<br/><br/><i>“I wish I could distinguish the defining moment we became more than…Just more.”</i><br/><br/>Annie has grown up wanting a “perfect” life, and nothing is going to stand in the way of her idea of that. She gets good grades and wants to find the perfect man f</span>
  <span id="freeText10370995915490907106" style="display:none"><b>*4.5 stars*<br /><br />**SHANYN’S REVIEW**</b><br /><br />I have never read a book by this author before, and after reading this one, I definitely plan on reading the others.<br /><br />Annie and Chase are wonderful together, they have such great chemistry, and I was drawn in right from the start.<br /><br /><i>“I wish I could distinguish the defining moment we became more than…Just more.”</i><br /><br />Annie has grown up wanting a “perfect” life, and nothing is going to stand in the way of her idea of that. She gets good grades and wants to find the perfect man for her future. She has known Chase since she was 14, and they have always had a love/hate relationship filled with sarcasm and pranks. But, there’s always been a hidden chemistry, that both deny.<br /><br /><i>“I don’t know how Chase does it. I don’t allow myself to envy him for too long, though. Chase is going nowhere fast and I shouldn’t admire that.”</i><br /><br />Chase is a laid back, tattoo covered, fun, loyal guy. He has no plan for the future, except to have fun and live in the moment. I loved Chase right from the start, with his jokes, flirting, and fun personality. I must admit I have a new book boyfriend.<br /><br /><i>“The thing is...I really do like Chase, like deep, deep down inside. I just hate how he makes me feel.”</i><br /><br />Annie has grown up feeling like she isn’t beautiful, and isn’t loved by anyone. Her mother is around, but they are not close. So, when Loden walks into her life and gives her the attention she is looking for, along with a perfect looking future, she thinks she has found the “perfect” man for her. When she quickly starts to find out Loden isn’t as “perfect” as she thinks he is, Chase is the man she always runs to, and the man that makes her feel safe and like “home”.<br /><br />Annie is such a wonderful, but closed off, girl who doesn’t want to end up like her mother. But, sometimes planning your perfect future, makes you miss the things right in front of you. This book was wonderful and filled with just enough angst to make my stomach roll every once in a while.<br /><br /><i>“I know there’s no way he’s aware of how I feel invisible most of the time and my need to make sure I’m seen. Remembered. But it’s almost like he put this song on just for me. Like it could have been written just for me.”</i><br /><br />I hated seeing Annie go through everything she did, but loved watching her emerge and learn from her experiences. Chase is there for Annie through it all, and seeing how patient he is with her, is beautiful.<br /><br /><i>“But when I decide I want something, I take it. Little motivates me, and it doesn’t happen often. She should feel special.”</i><br /><br />You will fall in love with Annie and Chase, their sarcasm, quick witted jokes, and chemistry.<br /><br /><i>“I get lost in my thoughts, trying to place exactly how today differs from yesterday. Or a month ago. Or a year ago. What’s scary is I can’t find it-that exact thing that changed.”</i><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10370995915490907106" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_650094883" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/650094883" />
    <a title="Dawn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6143839-dawn"><img alt="Dawn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1316710741p2/6143839.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/650094883?book_show_action=true">Jun 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dawn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dawn" href="/user/show/6143839-dawn">Dawn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer650094883" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4860209252522591124">Cheryl McIntyre has done it again. I loved Sometimes Never. I loved Before Now even more. But Long After is the bestest! And on a side note, Richard Rocco on the cover = H.O.T. I need the paperback to have the full pic of him! Anyhow...<br/><br/>Long After is told in both Chase and Annie's POV. The preface, in Chase's pov, is just...WOW! And all you can do is just wait for it. Chapter 2 is set twenty-seven months prior--their freshman year of college. From there on we learn what Chase and Annie's relation</span>
  <span id="freeText4860209252522591124" style="display:none">Cheryl McIntyre has done it again. I loved Sometimes Never. I loved Before Now even more. But Long After is the bestest! And on a side note, Richard Rocco on the cover = H.O.T. I need the paperback to have the full pic of him! Anyhow...<br /><br />Long After is told in both Chase and Annie's POV. The preface, in Chase's pov, is just...WOW! And all you can do is just wait for it. Chapter 2 is set twenty-seven months prior--their freshman year of college. From there on we learn what Chase and Annie's relationship was in the past, how it develops in college, and what happens to lead up to the event that occurs in the preface. And if you have read the other books in the series, Sometimes Never and Before Now, you will appreciate how Cheryl McIntyre folds all the storylines and characters together. (Don't worry if you have not read the other books. Long After can be read as a stand-alone.) <br /><br />The synopsis tells you exactly what the story is about. There really aren't to many secrets. What makes Cheryl's books--and specifically Long After, is the way Cheryl tells the story, the way she intertwines the storylines between the books, how realistic the plots are, and the way she develops her characters. And tho her books tackle serious subject matters, Cheryl writes in a way that balances these dark topics with light-hearted humor and witty banter. <br /><br />Per Chase, Annie is "an uptight, pain in the ass, with OCD tendancies, and a killer body." Per Chase, he is "an easygoing, loveable, slacker with a killer body." They have known each other since they were 14 and have been part of the same close-knit group of friends, tho Annie never really fit in. Once in college, what begins as a friendly rivalry--always trying to up one another, becomes something more--tho neither can name what that "more" is. "It's not friendship I feel for Annie, though I think it's safe to say she's my best friend." He knows Annie is looking for Mr. Perfect and he knows he is not what she perceives as perfect, but he is there anyways when she needs him most. He insists on nightly calls from Annie to make sure she's okay after he witnesses a situation between Annie and her "perfect" boyfriend, Loden, that makes him uncomfortable. This is how their relationship develops. Chase doesn't know how to tell Annie his feelings and he is always worried she will run from him, so he communicates thru music. (Awesome how Cheryl named each chapter after a song.) <br /><br />Long After is quite an emotional roller coaster. One minute you are laughing, the next you want to strangle someone, then you're swooning, anticipating, laughing again, cringing, crying....well, you get the point. Pick this book up...you won't regret it! </span>
  <a data-text-id="4860209252522591124" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer8906007799606992849">Safari crashed and deleted my lovely review. F-You Safari.<br/>Let me start off by saying that I was expecting so much more from this book, but it fell short for me. I loved Sometimes Never, it was a great book, and I couldn't get enough of it. Before Now shocked me, it surpassed my outstanding image of book #1, and it soon became one of my favorites, but this one appears to be lacking the flair that made the others so great. Typically, I got this novel the day it came out, so very eager to read the </span>
  <span id="freeText8906007799606992849" style="display:none">Safari crashed and deleted my lovely review. F-You Safari.<br />Let me start off by saying that I was expecting so much more from this book, but it fell short for me. I loved Sometimes Never, it was a great book, and I couldn't get enough of it. Before Now shocked me, it surpassed my outstanding image of book #1, and it soon became one of my favorites, but this one appears to be lacking the flair that made the others so great. Typically, I got this novel the day it came out, so very eager to read the next installment in this series, eager to once again be stunned, but I put it off... I've been putting it off because I've been having somewhat of a bad feeling about it... I hate when I'm right.<br />I don't know what to say.... this book was disappointing. I felt like the story was rushed, there was too much jumping around and not enough evaluation.. I didn't like how much time elapsed with nothing really being told.<br />I guess I simply don't get the plot..... why stay with someone who is abusive when a) you don't have kids b) you don't live together c) he isn't blackmailing you d) you have a decent enough support system to help you d) you see it for what its worth and CHOOSE not to do anything....... I just don't get it. I haven't been in a situation like that myself so I could be judging this harshly, but still.. it didn't seem right.<br />Annie was a really lame character for me. I never really related to her... she proved to be shallow and weak consistently during the book and it simply got annoying. Well, that and her overbearing OCD.. I GET IT, YOU'RE CREEPILY ORDERLY, GOOD FOR YOU, SHUT UP ALREADY....<br />This book was lacking for me... majorly. I wish this book continued with either Hope/Mason or Lucy/Park instead of new characters.. it would've made for a better read. I guess I'll label this as my first disappointment for 2014, because I really was expecting so much more. :/</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/679608789" />
    <a title="Ash" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15649398-ash"><img alt="Ash" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380921492p2/15649398.jpg" /></a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer679608789" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10044742680382314498">Blew me away. I have no idea where to begin...<br/><br/>This was amazing. I loved Chase and Annie, they were such an adorable couple. Chase just stole my heart from the beginning. "Nice guys usually lose" as is said in the beginning of the novel, and yet even as he struggled through his loses he kept his smile and his easy-going demeanor. He is perfect for Annie, and as was recognized, it was a shame she didn't realize it sooner. <br/><br/>I really liked the organization of this one. The leaps forward so you could </span>
  <span id="freeText10044742680382314498" style="display:none">Blew me away. I have no idea where to begin...<br /><br />This was amazing. I loved Chase and Annie, they were such an adorable couple. Chase just stole my heart from the beginning. "Nice guys usually lose" as is said in the beginning of the novel, and yet even as he struggled through his loses he kept his smile and his easy-going demeanor. He is perfect for Annie, and as was recognized, it was a shame she didn't realize it sooner. <br /><br />I really liked the organization of this one. The leaps forward so you could see the damage of whatever the climax was, way before it happened. It was interesting any it kept the story moving when it had the potential (since the story took place over the course of twenty-seven months) to be slow. It was in no way slow. Not one single part of it. <br /><br />I'm trying to think of something I didn't like, other than the main antagonist of course, but I'm coming up short. <br /><br />Okay, the inevitable, 'which of this series is my favorite so far?' Hmmm..... I have no idea. This one is beautiful, it showed so much emotion and the issues were so realistic and I love Chase....but there's just something about Before Now that really hooked me....I don't know. I think it might be a tie. Maybe. I don't know. I'd have to read them both over and over again. Which ever I get tired of first loses. (That'll take a long-ass time, so don't hold your breath for the results.)<br /><br />Five stars. It was amazing. Absolutely so. <br />p.s. I <i>loved</i> this cover. </span>
  <a data-text-id="10044742680382314498" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('vDlSQQeS14nwBCypnA9C0Wzq6OqHLvqty0hZ0qEVTZy+aGyWuXRIlk9xpyxUtrCCUGxL64V/5bl64oIPjPDabw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }
